and</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:13.8pt">$2.3 million in a first lien senior secured loan, $0.5 million in a first lien senior secured revolver and $0.7 million in a first lien senior secured delayed draw loan to a provider of janitorial services for the food distribution and grocery end markets.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">As of December&#160;31, 2024, MSC Income&#8217;s private loan portfolio included total investments at cost of approximately $697.5</font><font style="color:#ff0000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">million across 84 unique companies. MSC Income&#8217;s portfolio investments are typically made to support leveraged buyouts, recapitalizations, growth financings, refinancings and acquisitions of companies that operate in diverse industry sectors. MSC Income seeks to partner with private equity fund sponsors and primarily invests in secured debt investments within its private loan investment strategy. MSC Income seeks to partner with entrepreneurs, business owners and management teams and generally provides customized &#8220;one-stop&#8221; debt and equity financing solutions within its lower middle market investment strategy. MSC Income&#8217;s private loan portfolio companies generally have annual revenues between $25 million and $500 million. MSC Income&#8217;s lower middle market portfolio companies generally have annual revenues between $10 million and $150 million.</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:174%">ABOUT MSC ADVISER I, LLC</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">MSC Adviser I, LLC is a wholly owned subsidiary of Main Street Capital Corporation (NYSE&#58; MAIN) that is registered as an investment adviser under the Investment Advisers Act of 1940, as amended.
